Senior Business Analyst

2Base Technologies Pvt Ltd
Infopark

Senior Business Analyst role at 2Base requiring 4+ years of experience. Focus on functional modeling, requirement clarity, and end-to-end ownership to drive aligned product delivery.

4+ YearsSaaSAPIBRD/FRD/SRS
Apply by: 31 Jan 2026

Senior Business Analyst

At 2Base, we are rebuilding the Business Analyst function into a world-class, product-minded, clarity-driven team. This role is not a documentation role. It is not a screen updater role. It is not a support role. This is a core Business Analyst position responsible for functional modeling, system reasoning, requirement clarity, and building the foundation for correct development.

Key Responsibilities

  • Lead requirement workshops, client calls, and discovery discussions to understand business needs clearly.
  • Ask deeper questions, challenge assumptions, and validate the true business intent behind every requirement.
  • Convert ambiguous client inputs into structured, logical, and actionable functional understanding.
  • Break large features into modules, workflows, components, and clear dependencies.
  • Build strong system-level understanding involving APIs, integrations, data flow, and backend considerations.
  • Translate business processes into functional logic that development teams can execute.
  • Decompose requirements into use-case flows, system behaviors, edge cases, alternate paths, validation rules, and dependencies.
  • Prepare high-quality documentation, including BRD, FRD, SRS, workflows, state diagrams, data-flow diagrams, API requirement specs, and acceptance criteria.
  • Ensure all documentation is clear, logical, structured, testable, and ready for developers and QA to use.
  • Collaborate closely with developers, architects, QA, and product owners to validate feasibility and align understanding.
  • Ensure QA teams can derive test cases effectively from your functional logic and acceptance criteria.
  • Communicate confidently with clients, handle requirement discussions smoothly, and clarify misunderstandings immediately.
  • Push back politely on unclear or changing requirements and ensure final decisions are documented properly.
  • Maintain requirement traceability throughout the lifecycle and ensure zero ambiguity during handover to development.
  • Own the entire requirement lifecycle from discovery to development readiness with high accountability.
  • Drive clarity across teams by ensuring every requirement is complete, validated, and logically consistent.

Required Skills & Experience

  • Minimum 4+ years of core Business Analyst experience with strong analytical and system-level thinking.
  • Ability to break down complex requirements into clear components, workflows, and functional logic.
  • Excellent verbal and written communication with confidence in client interactions and clarifications.
  • Proven experience in preparing SRS, BRD, FRD, workflows, and acceptance criteria with high clarity.
  • Ability to challenge assumptions politely, ask the right questions, and ensure zero ambiguity.
  • Strong collaboration experience with development, QA, architects, and cross-functional teams.
  • Understanding of API behaviors, integrations, data flows, and multi-module system interactions.
  • Ability to run requirement discussions, workshops, and independently lead discovery sessions.
  • Exposure to SaaS, scalable products, automation, or AI-supported systems is an added advantage.
  • Demonstrated ownership of requirements end-to-end, ensuring developer-ready and testable outputs.
  • Not suitable for UI-only thinkers, passive communicators, template-based writers, or those relying on AI for answers.
  • Success is defined by clear, testable requirements, zero rework, strong cross-team alignment, and confident communication.

Minimum Qualifications

  • Bachelor’s degree in Computer Science, Engineering, Business, or related field
  • 4 to 8 years of experience as a Business Analyst or Product Analyst
  • Experience in SaaS or scalable product environments
  • Exposure to AI/Automation, integrations, or multi-module systems
  • Ability to run independent client workshops
  • Must have independently handled requirement ownership for at least one full project lifecycle

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

Contact: If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at careers@2basetechnologies.com.

Apply by: 31 Jan 2026

Business Analyst

The Business Analyst plays a key role in ensuring requirements are clearly understood, accurately documented, and traceable throughout the software development lifecycle. This role focuses on translating business and functional inputs into structured, standardized documentation that supports effective development, testing, and delivery. Working closely with business analysts, design teams, and technical stakeholders, the role ensures consistency, clarity, and alignment across all requirement artifacts.

Key Responsibilities

  • Create Software Requirement Specifications (SRS) based on inputs from Core Business Analysts, stakeholder discussions, and requirement walkthroughs
  • Prepare Business Requirement Documents (BRD) using approved templates while ensuring business intent and system behavior are clearly documented
  • Participate in requirement discussions to understand business objectives, functional flows, dependencies, and assumptions before documentation
  • Analyze requirements to identify gaps, ambiguities, and inconsistencies, and work with Core BAs to resolve them
  • Document functional flows, business rules, and acceptance criteria where applicable to support development and QA teams
  • Document wireframes, UI flows, validations, and UI specifications in collaboration with design and product teams
  • Maintain change logs, version history, and document updates throughout the project lifecycle
  • Create and manage traceability matrices linking business, functional, and technical requirements
  • Maintain cross-references across BRD, SRS, UI, API, and related documentation
  • Ensure documentation consistency, completeness, and alignment with approved scope and delivery timelines
  • Ensure accurate and timely PMS updates with structured documentation details
  • Support development, QA, UAT, and audit processes through clear, traceable, and up-to-date documentation
  • Assist in requirement reviews, walkthroughs, and validation sessions with internal and client stakeholders

Requirements

Required Skills and Experience

  • 1 to 4 years of experience in Business Analysis documentation or related roles
  • Strong experience in BRD and SRS creation
  • Hands-on experience with documentation templates, standards, and version control
  • Ability to document UI wireframes and functional flows clearly
  • Working knowledge of APIs and system integrations for documentation purposes
  • Experience with project management systems and documentation tools
  • Strong attention to detail and ability to manage multiple documents in parallel
  • Excellent written communication and stakeholder coordination skills

Minimum Qualifications

  • Bachelor’s degree in Engineering, Computer Science, Information Systems, or a related field

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

DevOps Engineer (AWS & On-Prem)

We are seeking a DevOps Engineer to design, build, and operate reliable, secure, and cost-efficient infrastructure across AWS and on-premises environments. This hands-on, leadership-oriented role requires expertise in infrastructure provisioning, system reliability, CI/CD orchestration, container platforms, security controls, and cost optimization.

Key Responsibilities

Infrastructure & Platform Engineering - Design, provision, and manage infrastructure across AWS and on-prem environments using Infrastructure as Code (IaC). - Provision and manage Linux-based servers, virtual machines, and bare-metal systems. - Configure and manage network components including VPCs, subnets, routing, firewalls, load balancers, VPNs, and network switches (on-prem). - Lead setup and maintenance of PostgreSQL databases, including backups, replication, performance tuning, and high availability.

Containerization & Orchestration - Design, deploy, and operate Kubernetes clusters (EKS and/or self-managed). - Build and maintain Docker-based container workflows. - Manage Kubernetes workloads, namespaces, ingress, secrets, autoscaling, and rolling deployments. - Establish best practices for container security, image scanning, and runtime hardening.

CI/CD & Automation - Design and maintain CI/CD pipelines for application and infrastructure code. - Orchestrate automated builds, tests, deployments, and rollbacks. - Implement GitOps or pipeline-driven deployment strategies. - Write and maintain automation scripts using Bash, Python, or similar scripting languages.

Monitoring, Reliability & Operations - Implement system monitoring, logging, and alerting for infrastructure and applications. - Define and track SLIs/SLOs and lead incident response and root cause analysis. - Ensure high availability, fault tolerance, and disaster recovery readiness. - Lead operational runbooks and on-call best practices.

Security & Compliance - Implement infrastructure and platform security best practices. - Manage IAM, secrets, encryption, network security, and access controls. - Support vulnerability management, patching, and audit readiness. - Collaborate with security teams to align with compliance and governance requirements.

Cost Optimization & Performance - Monitor and optimize AWS cloud spend using cost visibility and reporting tools. - Identify opportunities for rightsizing, reserved instances, autoscaling, and storage optimization. - Track on-prem infrastructure utilization and capacity planning. - Balance performance, reliability, and cost trade-offs.

Leadership & Collaboration - Act as a technical lead and mentor for DevOps engineers. - Define DevOps standards, best practices, and documentation. - Partner with engineering teams to improve developer experience and deployment velocity. - Participate in architecture discussions and infrastructure roadmap planning.

Required Qualifications

  • 3+ years of hands-on experience in DevOps, SRE, or Platform Engineering roles.
  • Strong experience with AWS (EC2, VPC, IAM, RDS, EKS, S3, CloudWatch, etc.).
  • Proven experience managing on-prem infrastructure (servers, virtualization, networking).
  • Deep Linux system administration experience.
  • Hands-on experience with PostgreSQL administration.
  • Strong knowledge of Docker and Kubernetes.
  • Experience with CI/CD tools and infrastructure automation.
  • Proficiency in scripting (Bash, Python, or similar).

Data Modeling & Transformation - Build Bronze → Silver → Gold data transformation pipelines - Implement Slowly Changing Dimensions (SCD2) to track historical changes - Design dimension and fact tables optimized for analytics and traceability - Implement data quality tests, documentation, and automated lineage tracking - Optimize partitioning, compression, and query performance

Serving & Access Patterns - Populate relational databases with aggregated metrics (e.g., velocity, defect rates, test coverage) - Implement graph data models for traceability (requirements ↔ code ↔ tests ↔ releases) - Build search indices for full-text queries (code commits, requirements, incidents) - Design APIs or views for downstream consumers (dashboards, agents)

Orchestration & Monitoring - Implement workflow orchestration (DAGs) with dependency management, retries, SLAs - Build observability into pipelines: metrics (latency, row counts, failures), logs, lineage diagrams - Create data quality dashboards and alerting (freshness, completeness, schema drift) - Document runbooks for incident response and troubleshooting

Infrastructure & Security - Provision cloud infrastructure using Infrastructure as Code (Terraform, CloudFormation, Pulumi) - Implement least-privilege IAM, VPC security, secrets management, encryption at rest/in transit - Design cost-efficient architectures (storage lifecycle policies, compute right-sizing, query optimization) - Ensure compliance with data governance and GDPR/ASPICE requirements - Set up CI/CD for infrastructure and pipeline code (GitHub Actions, GitLab CI, Azure DevOps)

Preferred Skills

Experience - 7+ years in data engineering roles, with at least 2 years building lakehouse architectures (Bronze/Silver/Gold or equivalent medallion patterns) - Proven track record delivering production-grade data platforms supporting 50+ data sources and 100+ users - Experience with graph databases (Neo4j, Amazon Neptune, TigerGraph) for relationship modeling - Hands-on with stream processing (Kafka, Flink, Spark Streaming, Kinesis)

Technical Skills (Core) - Cloud Platforms: Deep expertise in AWS, Azure, or GCP data services (S3/Blob, RDS/SQL Database, managed Kafka, serverless compute) - SQL & Data Modeling: Expert-level SQL, dimensional modeling, SCD2, normalization vs. denormalization trade-offs - Transformation Tools: dbt, Databricks SQL, Dataform, or custom SQL/Python frameworks - Programming: Python or Scala for data processing, scripting, and automation - Orchestration: Airflow, Prefect, Dagster, Step Functions, or Azure Data Factory - IaC: Terraform, CloudFormation, Pulumi, or ARM templates

Technical Skills (Preferred) - Search: OpenSearch, Elasticsearch, or Solr for text indexing and retrieval - Graph: Neo4j Cypher, SPARQL, or Gremlin for graph queries; experience with graph ETL - Data Quality: Great Expectations, dbt tests, or custom validation frameworks - Real-time: Flink, Spark Streaming, or serverless event processing (Lambda, Cloud Functions) - Monitoring: Grafana, Datadog, or CloudWatch for data pipeline observability
